By analysing your preferences, budget, and desired features, Soho generates personalised property recommendations that cater to your unique needs, making the search for <a href="/matches/buy">houses for sale</a> and <strong>rental properties</strong> simpler and more enjoyable.</p><br/><h3>Frequently Asked Questions About the Australian Property Market</h3><div class="style_faq__Iljza"><div class="style_collapsible__eYbHI"><div class="style_question__Q7ff2"><h4>Is it good time to buy property?</h4><div class="style_arrow__aEWty"><img src="/_nextassets/icons/back_706F73.svg" alt="arrow" width="24" height="24"/></div></div><div class="style_answer___T5nE"><p>It is difficult to say whether it is a good time to buy property. The answer depends on a number of factors, including your individual circumstances, the state of the property market, and your long-term investment goals. If you are looking to buy a property to live in, then it is important to consider your financial situation and your needs.</p><br/><p>Can you afford the monthly repayments on the <a href="/mortgage-calculator">home loan</a>? Do you have enough saved for a deposit? And is the property in a location that you want to live in?</p><br/><p>If you are looking to buy a property as an investment, then you need to consider the potential rental income and capital growth. Can you afford to hold the property for a long period of time? And are you comfortable with the risk of the property market? These are the types of questions to ask yourself when <a href="/articles/buying-your-first-home-in-australia">buying a home in Australia</a>.</p></div></div><div class="style_collapsible__eYbHI"><div class="style_question__Q7ff2"><h4>Where is the cheapest place for property in Australia?</h4><div class="style_arrow__aEWty"><img src="/_nextassets/icons/back_706F73.svg" alt="arrow" width="24" height="24"/></div></div><div class="style_answer___T5nE"><p>The cheapest place for property in Australia depends on factors like region, property type, and market conditions. Use Soho&#x27;s search filters and expert advice to find affordable properties across the country. Some of the <a href="/articles/10-of-the-cheapest-houses-in-australia">cheapest houses in Australia</a> can be found in regional areas of South Australia and Queensland.</p></div></div><div class="style_collapsible__eYbHI"><div class="style_question__Q7ff2"><h4>Will this year be a good time to buy a house in Australia?</h4><div class="style_arrow__aEWty"><img src="/_nextassets/icons/back_706F73.svg" alt="arrow" width="24" height="24"/></div></div><div class="style_answer___T5nE"><p>Property market conditions can change, making it difficult to predict the ideal time to <a href="/articles/how-to-buy-a-house-in-australia">buy a house in Australia</a>. Stay informed with Soho&#x27;s market insights and expert advice to help you make the best decision for your circumstances.</p></div></div><div class="style_collapsible__eYbHI"><div class="style_question__Q7ff2"><h4>Why are houses so expensive in Australia?</h4><div class="style_arrow__aEWty"><img src="/_nextassets/icons/back_706F73.svg" alt="arrow" width="24" height="24"/></div></div><div class="style_answer___T5nE"><p>There are a number of reasons why houses are so expensive in Australia. Some of the most common reasons include:</p><br/><ul><li>Strong population growth: Australia&#x27;s population has been growing steadily for many years, which puts upward pressure on house prices.</li><li>Investor demand: Many people invest in property in Australia, which drives up demand and prices.</li><li>Government policies: Some government policies, such as negative gearing, can make it more attractive to invest in property, which can drive up prices.</li></ul><br/><p>It is important to note that these are just some of the reasons why houses are expensive in Australia. The exact reasons vary depending on the location and the <a href="/articles/different-housing-types-explained">type of property</a>.</p></div></div><div class="style_collapsible__eYbHI"><div class="style_question__Q7ff2"><h4>Average Rent in Australia</h4><div class="style_arrow__aEWty"><img src="/_nextassets/icons/back_706F73.svg" alt="arrow" width="24" height="24"/></div></div><div class="style_answer___T5nE"><p>The <a href="/articles/average-rent-in-australia">average rent in Australia</a> varies depending on the city or town, but it is generally quite high. In Sydney, for example, the average rent for a one-bedroom apartment is much higher while Melbourne has some of the cheapest rent in Australia amongst capital cities.</p></div></div><div class="style_collapsible__eYbHI"><div class="style_question__Q7ff2"><h4>Why is Rent so Expensive in Australia?</h4><div class="style_arrow__aEWty"><img src="/_nextassets/icons/back_706F73.svg" alt="arrow" width="24" height="24"/></div></div><div class="style_answer___T5nE"><p>The population is growing rapidly, which puts pressure on the supply of <a href="/matches/rent">rental properties</a>. The <a href="/articles/what-it-costs-to-build-a-house-in-2021">cost of building new homes</a> is high, which also drives up rents. Government policies, such as negative gearing, can make it more attractive to invest in property, which can also increase rents. In order to stay competitive, renters should know <a href="/articles/how-to-describe-yourself-to-a-landlord-examples">how to describe yourself to the landlord</a> and maximise chances of securing rentals.</p></div></div><div class="style_collapsible__eYbHI"><div class="style_question__Q7ff2"><h4>Is it Cheaper to Rent or Buy in Australia?</h4><div class="style_arrow__aEWty"><img src="/_nextassets/icons/back_706F73.svg" alt="arrow" width="24" height="24"/></div></div><div class="style_answer___T5nE"><p>It is difficult to say definitively whether it is cheaper to <a href="/articles/renting-vs-buying">rent or buy in Australia</a>. The answer will vary depending on your individual circumstances, such as your income, your deposit savings, and your location. However, in general, it is becoming more difficult for people to afford to buy a home in Australia, so renting may be a more affordable option for some people.</p></div></div></div></section><div respectful of property. Crafting a compelling renter profile, complete with a cover letter and renter resume, can showcase these qualities effectively. \u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eIn this guide, you’ll find \u003cstrong\u003epractical examples and expert tips \u003c/strong\u003eto help you create a polished and persuasive rental application.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003ch2\u003eHow to Describe Yourself to a Landlord: Examples\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eA well-crafted description can help you win over a landlord. Here are some \u003cstrong\u003eexamples\u003c/strong\u003e of what to say about yourself:\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eResponsible and Reliable\u003c/strong\u003e: \u0026#8220;As a tenant, I pride myself on being responsible and reliable. I always pay my rent on time and ensure that the property is well-maintained.\u0026#8221;\u003c/li\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eOrganized and Clean\u003c/strong\u003e: \u0026#8220;I am a very organized and clean person. I keep my living space tidy and make sure to follow all cleaning guidelines provided.\u0026#8221;\u003c/li\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRespectful and Considerate\u003c/strong\u003e: \u0026#8220;I value respect and consideration, especially in a shared community. I’m mindful of noise levels and courteous to neighbors.\u0026#8221;\u003c/li\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eExcellent Communication Skills\u003c/strong\u003e: \u0026#8220;I have excellent communication skills and am prompt in responding to landlord queries. Open communication is key to maintaining a positive relationship.\u0026#8221;\u003c/li\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFinancial Stability\u003c/strong\u003e: \u0026#8220;I have a steady income and am able to provide proof of employment and income verification. Rent payments will always be a top priority for me.\u0026#8221;\u003c/li\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eNon-Smoker and No Pets\u003c/strong\u003e: \u0026#8220;I am a non-smoker and do not have any pets, ensuring there won’t be any disruptions or potential damages.\u0026#8221;\u003c/li\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eLong-Term Tenant\u003c/strong\u003e: \u0026#8220;I am looking for a long-term rental to call home. I value stability and look forward to building a positive relationship with my landlord.\u0026#8221;\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eFor more details on \u003cstrong\u003equalities that appeal to a landlord\u003c/strong\u003e, check out this article on \u003ca href=\"https://soho.com.au/articles/what-qualities-does-the-applicant-have-which-would-be-appealing-to-a-landlord\"\u003ewhat qualities does the applicant have which would be appealing to a landlord\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003ch2\u003eCover Letter Examples for Tenants\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cfigure class=\"wp-block-image size-full\"\u003e\u003cimg decoding=\"async\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"402\" src=\"data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAAAAACH5BAEKAAEALAAAAAABAAEAAAICTAEAOw==\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-51549 lazyload\" data-src=\"https://soho.com.au/articles/wp-content/uploads/2025/02/What-does-17-2-768x402-1.webp\"\u003e\u003c/figure\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eCrafting a strong cover letter for your rental application can make all the difference. Here are two examples to help you stand out:\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003ch3\u003eRenter Cover Letter Example 1: Standard Tenant Without Pets\u003c/h3\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003e\u0026#8220;Dear Mr./Ms. Landlord,\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003eI’m writing to express my interest in your property at [address]. I have been a tenant in [city] for the past five years and have a clean rental history. Currently, I am employed as a [job title] at [company name], and I have a stable income.\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003eI am a reliable and responsible tenant, paying rent on time and maintaining the property well. I’m also respectful and quiet, and I believe I would make an excellent tenant.\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003eI have attached my rental application and references and would be happy to answer any questions you may have. Thank you for your time and consideration.\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003eSincerely, [Your Name]\u0026#8221;\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eFor more tips on making your rental application stand out, visit this article on \u003ca href=\"https://soho.com.au/articles/how-can-i-make-my-rental-application-stand-out\"\u003ehow can I make my rental application stand out\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003ch3\u003eRenter Cover Letter Example 2: Tenant with a Pet\u003c/h3\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003e\u0026#8220;Dear [Landlord’s Name],\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003eI’m writing to express my interest in [property address]. Your property seems like a great fit.\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003eI’ve been employed as a [job title] at [company name] for the last [number of years/months], and I take pride in being a respectful tenant. My pet is well-behaved and fully vaccinated, and I understand the responsibilities that come with pet ownership.\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003eI’m happy to provide references and am open to discussing a pet deposit. I look forward to hearing from you and hope to arrange a meeting soon.\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003eSincerely, [Your Name]\u0026#8221;\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003ch2\u003eHow to Craft a Winning Renter Resume\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cfigure class=\"wp-block-image size-full\"\u003e\u003cimg decoding=\"async\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"768\" height=\"512\" src=\"data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAAAAACH5BAEKAAEALAAAAAABAAEAAAICTAEAOw==\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-51550 lazyload\" data-src=\"https://soho.com.au/articles/wp-content/uploads/2025/02/pexels-karolina-grabowska-5387258-2-768x512-1.webp\"\u003e\u003c/figure\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eA \u003cstrong\u003erenter resume\u003c/strong\u003e is a great way to present yourself to potential landlords. Here’s how to put one together:\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003col\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eObjective Statement\u003c/strong\u003e: State what you\u0026#8217;re looking for in a rental and why you’re a great fit.\u003c/li\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePersonal Information\u003c/strong\u003e: Include your full name, contact details, and relevant information like whether you have pets.\u003c/li\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eEmployment History\u003c/strong\u003e: Showcase your job stability and income to prove you can meet rent payments. Be transparent and list your experience accurately.\u003c/li\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eReferences\u003c/strong\u003e: Provide at least two references who can vouch for your reliability as a tenant.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eFor more examples of \u003cstrong\u003ehow to share details about your rental history\u003c/strong\u003e, take a look at this \u003ca href=\"https://soho.com.au/articles/please-share-a-few-details-about-your-history-as-a-renter-example\"\u003erenter history example\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003ch2\u003eHow to Present a Strong Rental Application\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eIn today’s competitive rental market, a strong application can set you apart. Follow these steps:\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003col\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eBe Thorough\u003c/strong\u003e: Fill out every section of the application accurately. Missing details could slow down the process.\u003c/li\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTailor Your Application\u003c/strong\u003e: Mention features of the property that appeal to you and highlight why you\u0026#8217;re the perfect tenant.\u003c/li\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eProvide Documentation\u003c/strong\u003e: Attach your employment verification, rental history, and references.\u003c/li\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWrite a Cover Letter\u003c/strong\u003e: A brief but well-crafted cover letter can personalize your application and help you stand out. Use this guide on \u003ca href=\"https://soho.com.au/articles/rent-application-tips\"\u003erent application tips\u003c/a\u003e to learn more.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003ch2\u003eFinal Thoughts\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eDescribing yourself effectively to a landlord is about showcasing your strengths and presenting yourself as a reliable tenant. Whether it’s through a cover letter, a \u003cstrong\u003erenter resume\u003c/strong\u003e, or strong references, focus on qualities that landlords value the most. Remember to be clear, honest, and professional.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eIn a competitive rental market, presenting yourself well can make all the difference in securing your next home.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003chr class=\"wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity\"/\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003ch2\u003eFrequently Asked Questions on \u0026#8216;How to Describe Yourself to a Landlord\u0026#8217;\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003ch3\u003eWhat are some important qualities landlords look for in potential tenants?\u003c/h3\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eLandlords typically look for tenants who have a good credit score, stable employment, and a clean rental history. They also prefer tenants who are responsible, respectful, and can pay rent on time.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003ch3\u003eHow can I make a good first impression when introducing myself to a landlord?\u003c/h3\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eTo make a good first impression, dress appropriately and be on time for the appointment. Be polite and respectful, and show interest in the property. Answer questions honestly and provide references if requested.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003ch3\u003eWhat should I include in a letter of interest to rent a property?\u003c/h3\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eIn a letter of interest, include your name, contact information, and a brief introduction of yourself. Mention why you are interested in the property and what makes you a good candidate. Provide references and any other relevant information that may help you stand out.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003ch3\u003eCan you provide an example of a tenant bio that would impress a landlord?\u003c/h3\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026#8220;I am a responsible, reliable tenant with a stable job and excellent rental history. I take pride in maintaining a clean and tidy living space and always pay rent on time. \u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eI am also respectful of my neighbours and always follow the rules and regulations set by the landlord. I am confident that I would make an excellent tenant and take great care of your property.\u0026#8221;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003ch3\u003eWhat are some tips for selling myself to a landlord during a rental application process?\u003c/h3\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eBe honest and transparent about your rental history, employment, and financial situation. Provide references and any other relevant information that may help you stand out. Show interest in the property and ask questions to demonstrate your enthusiasm.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003ch3\u003eWhat should I say in an email to a landlord to express my interest in renting their property?\u003c/h3\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eIn an email, introduce yourself and express your interest in the property. Provide your contact information and ask any questions you may have. Thank the landlord for their time and consideration and express your willingness to provide any additional information they may need.\u003c/p\u003e\n","protected":false},"excerpt":{"rendered":"\u003cp\u003eLearn how to describe yourself to a landlord with practical examples and tips.
